Problem 1: 

(VAR vu95NonEmpty u x y z)
(THEORY 
(AC plus times))
(RULES
num0(S) -> S
abs(x) -> ifu95abs(x,x,S)
ifu95abs(num0(x),y,z) -> ifu95abs(x,y,z)
ifu95abs(num1(x),y,z) -> ifu95abs(x,y,num1(S))
ifu95abs(S,x,num1(S)) -> x
ifu95abs(S,x,S) -> S
ifu95abs(S,x,j(S)) -> opp(x)
ifu95abs(j(x),y,z) -> ifu95abs(x,y,j(S))
ifu95min(num0(x),y,z,u) -> ifu95min(x,y,z,u)
ifu95min(num1(x),y,z,u) -> ifu95min(x,y,z,num1(S))
ifu95min(S,x,y,num1(S)) -> x
ifu95min(S,x,y,S) -> x
ifu95min(S,x,y,j(S)) -> y
ifu95min(j(x),y,z,u) -> ifu95min(x,y,z,j(S))
ifu95sign(num0(x),y) -> ifu95sign(x,y)
ifu95sign(num1(x),y) -> ifu95sign(x,num1(S))
ifu95sign(S,x) -> x
ifu95sign(j(x),y) -> ifu95sign(x,j(S))
min(x,y) -> ifu95min(minus(abs(y),abs(x)),x,y,S)
minu39(x,y) -> ifu95min(minus(abs(num1(y)),abs(num1(x))),x,y,S)
minu39u39(x,y) -> ifu95min(minus(abs(j(y)),abs(j(x))),x,y,S)
minus(x,y) -> plus(opp(y),x)
opp(num0(x)) -> num0(opp(x))
opp(num1(x)) -> j(opp(x))
opp(S) -> S
opp(j(x)) -> num1(opp(x))
plus(num0(x),num0(y)) -> num0(plus(x,y))
plus(num0(x),num1(y)) -> num1(plus(x,y))
plus(num0(x),j(y)) -> j(plus(x,y))
plus(num1(x),num1(y)) -> j(plus(num1(S),plus(x,y)))
plus(num1(x),j(y)) -> num0(plus(x,y))
plus(S,x) -> x
plus(j(x),j(y)) -> num1(plus(j(S),plus(x,y)))
sign(x) -> ifu95sign(x,S)
times(num0(x),y) -> num0(times(x,y))
times(num1(x),y) -> plus(num0(times(x,y)),y)
times(S,x) -> S
times(j(x),y) -> minus(num0(times(x,y)),y)
)

 ifu95abs(j(x),y,z) -> ifu95abs(x,y,j(S))

 ifu95min(S,x,y,j(S)) -> y
 ifu95min(j(x),y,z,u) -> ifu95min(x,y,z,j(S))

 minu39u39(x,y) -> ifu95min(minus(abs(j(y)),abs(j(x))),x,y,S)
 minus(x,y) -> plus(opp(y),x)
 opp(num0(x)) -> num0(opp(x))
 opp(num1(x)) -> j(opp(x))
 opp(S) -> S
 opp(j(x)) -> num1(opp(x))
 plus(num0(x),num0(y)) -> num0(plus(x,y))
 plus(num0(x),num1(y)) -> num1(plus(x,y))
 plus(num0(x),j(y)) -> j(plus(x,y))
 plus(num1(x),num1(y)) -> j(plus(num1(S),plus(x,y)))
 plus(num1(x),j(y)) -> num0(plus(x,y))
 plus(S,x) -> x
 plus(j(x),j(y)) -> num1(plus(j(S),plus(x,y)))
 sign(x) -> ifu95sign(x,S)
 times(num0(x),y) -> num0(times(x,y))
 times(num1(x),y) -> plus(num0(times(x,y)),y)
 times(S,x) -> S
 times(j(x),y) -> minus(num0(times(x,y)),y)
